msg:Facilities:
Moving from Meijing Pavilion to this hotel, the difference is really big. Luneng has not been open for many years, and the maintenance is even worse than Wanda. The room price is more than 2,000, and the supporting facilities are only at the level of a four-star hotel. The hair dryer used is very stingy. The basin and toilet can also be seen to be of a relatively ordinary series.
Hygiene:
There is a layer of dust on the bedside table, and the hygiene is also very bad.
Noise:
It was more than 8 o'clock in the morning, and it was like a vegetable market outside. Children were running and adults were calling their companions loudly. The sound insulation was very poor. I put on noise-canceling headphones, but I could still hear the ringtone of the WeChat phone call outside. I thought I didn't close the door for a while. It was too outrageous.

I don't recommend this hotel at all. If you want to ski, Wanda's ski resort is more convenient and the ski slope is better. Luneng's largest slope ski slope can't catch up with Wanda's intermediate slope. It is really only suitable for novices.
If you have to stay in Luneng, I suggest choosing Meijing Pavilion. The price is not much different. It is simply a difference between heaven and earth. I can't imagine how the quality of hotels operated by Accor can be so different.

msg:Room
I originally thought that a twin bed room would be larger in size, but I was shocked when I stepped into the room. It was a twin bed suite ğŸ˜ƒ; the layout of the room is very reasonable, there is a sink near the cooking table near the entrance, and there is a four-bed suite in the room. Seat dining table, sofa, balcony, and of course a toilet. The bathroom area is also large, and it is very convenient to have a clothesline. The whole room has floor heating, so people who are afraid of the cold are not afraid at all.
spare parts
Toothbrushes, combs and other disposable supplies are complete. There are six bottles of water in the room, probably because the air is dry and you need to drink more water. This is much better than the two bottles of water in urban hotels.
landscape
The hotel is located in Luneng Resort Resort, 20 minutes by car from Changbai Airport and 1 hour and 20 minutes from the high-speed railway station. The natural oxygen bar in summer is enchanting in winter with its silver covering, the trees in autumn are full of autumn colors, and the mountains and mountains are only in the sunset. Nature has its own beauty, and it is the best color master.
Serve
Because it was an itinerary decided on a temporary basis, I called the front desk to see if I could arrange a pick-up after I made the reservation on the same day (although the terms require a one-day notice in advance), but the front desk was very happy to arrange it; the little brother who picked up the airport sent me a text message in advance to help Take the luggage and pick it up smoothly. Since the hotel is in the off-season, the included breakfast is delivered to the room, which not only eliminates waste, but also saves time, and one serving is enough. The restaurant service is also very good, especially the restaurant manager Carey, because it is inconvenient to buy things, I keep asking if there is anything I havenâ€™t brought. I can contact her; itâ€™s great to make friends while traveling!
Be sure to stay longer next time to feel the nature

In terms of environment, there is nothing wrong with Luneng's self-proclaimed little Switzerland. This year, it is Disney's anniversary celebration, and there are cooperative castle snow sculptures, etc. Luneng in the snow under the fireworks is simply a fairy tale town. ! !
In terms of matching, I have to give a thumbs up to Luneng's new EP! Similar to CM's GO, the team has just been established and is still very enthusiastic. The ski resort is enough for Xiaobai, but there is one thing to note: Luneng Ski Resort does not have a night course, and it ends at 15:00! We arranged to come to Xipo at the last stop, so that we could catch the plane the next day, but the check-in day was already past, so we had to get up early the next day and take the baby to experience it. If you donâ€™t ski, you can see Changbai Mountain by the cable car. Even if you take the cable car, the children will be very happyğŸ˜
In terms of facilities, it is not a new hotel after all, and there are still some minor problems, but the service wins. I booked a family suite, and it was almost 4 o'clock on the day of check-in. The room was still not cleaned up. I upgraded the villa type, but the sanitation was still relatively sloppy. I asked my aunt to help mop the floor again.
To sum it up is:
The scenery is beautiful (especially in snow season)
Great service (especially EP)
The food is delicious (especially Korean barbecue and seventh coffee)
The package is very good (especially EP, Xingqibao and Tongrentang physiotherapy)

posted:Posted August 16, 2022
msg:An unforgettable experience in the cool summer of Changbai Mountain beyond expectations
It is a rare opportunity to escape to Changbai Mountain in Northeast China during the summer vacation, and choosing a Swiss brand hotel under Accor Group is really an unforgettable experience.
The hotel is located in the Luneng Resort. Compared with the Changbai Mountain Wanda Tourist Resort, which was developed in the early days, it looks more secluded. As an Accor Platinum member, although I did not pass the official website, it was limited to a 65-square-meter villa with a big bed and free delivery. For the courtesy of the executive lounge, I really appreciate the warm and patient service at the front desk, and especially praise the front desk manager July for his personalized service and introduction to the surrounding area of the hotel;
The hotel is about a 20-minute drive from Changbaishan Airport. There are buses to the ancient city, Jinjiang Wooden House Village, Changbai Mountain West Scenic Area, etc. The hotel belongs to a Swiss brand. The entire architectural style and surrounding environment are very Swiss. Introducing the virgin forest of Changbai Mountain, quiet and peaceful, outdoor Taoyuan, blending into nature, cool summer, stunned, really in a certain Swiss town, if you are not afraid of cold and like skiing, it is highly recommended to stay here, then you can wait for winter Now, the average temperature in summer is 20-24 degrees, which is very suitable for summer vacation. The hotel is also a pet-friendly hotel, equipped with pet supplies. The hotel also has a number of children and adults venues, covering a number of sports facilities, all in person, feel the summer in Changbai activities, it is worth going to escape the heat this summer;
The rooms are simple, clean and comfortable. The villa rooms have independent balconies, and the view from the window can be seen. The wooden houses in front of you, the top of Changbai Mountain in the distance, and the surrounding mountains and fields have a panoramic view. Of course, if you stay in winter, you can also enjoy the snow-capped artistic conception on the top of the mountain. The room is very spacious and bright, the walls of the room are all spliced with original ecological wood, the furniture is also made of raw wood, and the whole room is full of reassuring wood aroma, very close to nature, really quite Swiss;
It's a little regrettable that there is no buffet in the evening, but you must taste the food and wine of Changbai Mountain in this hotel, especially the local wine of Changbai Mountain, which can be experienced in the red bar. Here, I nominated and praised the chef, Nie Tianhao, helped me make it. The special Northeastern cuisine is really refreshing and very Northeastern. Manager Guo also recommended to me about the special products of Changbai Mountain and the tasting of local special wines;
I hope to have the opportunity to take a Swiss-style summer vacation trip to Changbai Mountain.
